<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-.05pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
35.45pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Considerando o contido no <b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>processo nº 620/1999  volume 2</b>;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-.05pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span><span
style='letter-spacing:-.2pt'>considerando o disposto nas Resoluções n<sup>os</sup>
023/2000-CEP, 009/2004-CEP, 009/2005-CEP e 090/2005-CEP;<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>considerando o Parecer nº 138/2005 da Câmara de Graduação,
Extensão e Educação Básica e Profissional,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-.05pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>considerando
o disposto no Artigo 23 do Estatuto da Universidade Estadual de Maringá,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 style='text-indent:35.45pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>O CONSELHO DE ENSINO, PESQUISA E
EXTENSÃO APROVOU E EU, VICE-REITOR, NO USO DE MINHAS ATRIBUIÇÕES ESTATUTÁRIAS E
REGIMENTAIS, SANCIONO A SEGUINTE RESOLUÇÃO:<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=BodyText21 style='mso-pagination:none'><span style='font-family:Arial;
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";layout-grid-mode:line'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 1º</span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Fica alterada a nomenclatura
do componente curricular Projeto Final de Curso, do projeto pedagógico do <b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>curso de graduação em Engenharia Mecânica</b>,
para Trabalho de Conclusão de Curso.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 2º</span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Ficam aprovadas as
alterações no projeto pedagógico do referido curso, conforme <span
style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span>o Anexo I e o regulamento do componente
Estágio Curricular Supervisionado, conforme o Anexo II, partes integrantes
desta Resolução.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 3º </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>As alterações acima e o regulamento passam a vigorar no ano
letivo de 2006.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 4º<span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Esta
Resolução entra em vigor na data de sua publicação, revogadas as disposições em
contrário.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Dê-se ciência.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=BodyText21 style='mso-pagination:none'><span style='font-family:Arial;
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";layout-grid-mode:line'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Cumpra-se.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:8.0cm'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Maringá, 14 de dezembro de 2005.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>: 68 h/a teóricas, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>: 1º semestre da 4ª série;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Fundamentos teóricos e princípios de microeconomia e
macroeconomia. Elementos de engenharia econômica.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.3pt'>Objetivo(s):</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.3pt'> Compreender a importância da análise econômica, conhecer os critérios
de seleção de projetos de investimento e entender funcionamento básico do
mercado de capitais.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Economia<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><span style='font-size:8.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>ADMINISTRAÇÃO PARA ENGENHARIA
MECÂNICA</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 68 h/a teóricas <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 1º semestre da 5ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.3pt'>Ementa:</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.3pt'>
Compreender a relevância e aplicação dos conhecimentos de administração da
produção, organização industrial, planejamento e controle da produção,
gerenciamento de projetos, qualidade e produtividade e normas de conformidade
nos sistemas produtivos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Objetivo(s):</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Permitir o debate da aplicação prática dos conceitos e
técnicas de administração da produção diante de um contexto social e econômico.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Administração<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><span style='font-size:8.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:0cm;text-indent:0cm;mso-outline-level:

"Times New Roman"'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>alteração da
nomenclatura, ementa e objetivos das disciplinas:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><u><span style='font-size:

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária:</span></b><span

"Times New Roman"'> 68 h/a teóricas<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

"Times New Roman"'> 3ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> Sistemas e dispositivos utilizados em equipamentos
elétricos e eletrônicos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> <span style='color:black'>Utilizar os conceitos
fundamentais de eletrotécnica e eletrônica no dimensionamento de máquinas e

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><span style='font-size:8.0pt;

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><u><span style='font-size:

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

"Times New Roman"'> 3ª série<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> Sistemas de geração e aproveitamento de energia térmica<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

térmicos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

<p class=MsoBodyText style='mso-outline-level:7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Conceitos fundamentais e aplicações envolvendo os processos
de transferência de quantidade de movimento e calor.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.2pt'>Objetivo(s):</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.2pt'> Compreender e solucionar problemas na área de Engenharia Mecânica que
envolvam balanços integrais e diferenciais de transferência de qualidade de
movimento e calor.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;text-indent:
0cm;mso-outline-level:7;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list 18.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>4.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>alteração da
nomenclatura, carga horária, seriação, ementa e objetivos das disciplinas:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><u><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Dinâmica de Máquinas e Mecanismos</span></u><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> para <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>MECANISMOS</b>,
<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga Horária:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> de 136h/a para 68 h/a teóricas <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação: </span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span>3ª série para o 2º
semestre da 4ª série <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa: </span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Análise gráfica de velocidades e acelerações . Introdução à
síntese de mecanismos. Análise cinemática e dinâmica de mecanismos articulados
espaciais.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Objetivo(s):</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Analisar mecanismos planos e espaciais em seus aspectos
cinemáticos e dinâmicos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>: Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;mso-outline-level:7;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list 18.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>5.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>remanejamento da
disciplina <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>TERMODINÂMICA</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> (1519) <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 136 h/a<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>3ª série para 2ª
série <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Leis da Termodinâmica e suas aplicações<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Compreender os princípios fundamentais da termodinâmica e
aplicá-los na solução de problemas<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>de
Engenharia Mecânica.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:

"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:

"Times New Roman"'>6.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>criação da disciplina
<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:

FLUIDOTÉRMICA <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 3ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Práticas em Termodinâmica, Mecânica dos Fluídos e
Transferência de Calor.<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Verificar os princípios de Termodinâmica, Mecânica dos
Fluídos e Transferência de Calor confrontando teoria e prática.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span

"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

SISTEMAS FLUIDOMECÂNICOS</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 68 h/a práticas  anual<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>4ª série, anual<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Identificação, classificação e dimensionamento de
componentes dos sistemas hidráulicos e pneumáticos. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

MATERIAIS,<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 3ª série <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa: </span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Ensaios aplicados para a caracterização das propriedades
mecânicas e estruturais dos materiais de construção mecânica.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Objetivo(s)</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>: Interpretar os resultados obtidos de ensaios aplicados em
materiais utilizados na construção de elementos mecânicos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:
</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamento de Engenharia
Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>FABRICAÇÃO
MECÂNICA,<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga Horária:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 136 h/a práticas - anual,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 4ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>: Práticas em processos de fabricação por usinagem,
processos metalúrgicos e de conformação mecânica. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Objetivo(s):</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Aplicar os processos de manufatura na fabricação de
elementos e sistemas mecânicos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>PROJETO EM
ENGENHARIA MECÂNICA</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>: 68 h/a teóricas<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>2º semestre da 4º
série, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";color:black'> Concepção, projeto preliminar, planejamento e
estudo de viabilidade de projetos em Engenharia Mecânica</span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Objetivo(s)</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>:<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>Desenvolver o
potencial criativo e crítico na elaboração de um projeto na área de engenharia
mecânica.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:

"Times New Roman"'>7.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>alteração de carga
horária, ementa e objetivos <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>SISTEMAS
HIDRÁULICOS E PNEUMÁTICOS</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> 102 h/a para 68 h/a teóricas<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> 4ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Sistemas de engenharia controlados por meio de dispositivos
hidráulicos e/ou pneumáticos e os elementos q o compõem.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Identificar, dimensionar e projetar sistemas
fluidomecânicos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:

style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span

"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

CONCLUSÃO DE CURSO <o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> <span style='color:black'>Trabalho de síntese e integração
dos conhecimentos adquiridos ao longo do curso.<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:black'>Objetivo(s):</span></b><span

"Times New Roman";color:black'> </span><span style='font-size:11.5pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Desenvolver
um projeto na área de engenharia mecânica.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> 204 h/a para 170 h/a teóricas - anual;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> 4ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> Processamento de materiais de engenharia por usinagem, conformação
mecânica, métodos metalúrgicos e outros métodos de fabricação.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

"Times New Roman"'> Selecionar os processos de fabricação adequados para a
manufatura de elementos e sistemas mecânicos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b

10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>: Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>MÁQUINAS DE
FLUXO<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>: 102 h/a para 68 h/a teóricas  anual<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> 4ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Definição, classificação e dimensionamento de componentes
que compõem um sistema de transporte de fluídos.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Objetivo(s):</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Projetar e especificar sistemas com máquinas de fluxo e
otimizar potências e rendimentos dessas instalações.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>MATERIAIS DE
CONSTRUÇÃO MECÂNICA</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária:
</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes"> </span>136 h/a teóricas  anual<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação: </span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>3ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Princípios de Ciência e engenharia de materiais aplicados
na construção de elementos ou sistemas mecânicos<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Objetivo(s):</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Identificar as principais propriedades dos materiais,
associando-as à estrutura interna do material e aos defeitos nesta estrutura,
além de empregar técnicas a fim de obter informações acerca das suas
propriedades mecânicas.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Departamento de Engenharia Química<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>ELEMENTOS DE
MÁQUINAS<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>de 136 h/a para 102
h/a teóricas, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>1º semestre da 4º
série, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ementa: </span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Fundamentos de Projetos de Máquinas. Eixos, Mancais, Soldas,
Engrenagens, Molas, Embreagem e Freios. Transmissões Flexíveis<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Objetivo(s): </span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";color:black'>Projetar, dimensionar e selecionar elementos de
máquinas com base na solicitação/tensão, resistência/critérios e segurança do
componente.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:black'>Departamentalização:</span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";color:black'> Departamento de Engenharia Química</span><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span
style='font-size:8.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-18.0pt;mso-outline-level:7;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo4;tab-stops:list 18.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>8.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>alteração de carga
horária e seriação <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>ELETROTÉCNICA
E ELETRÔNICA APLICADA</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Carga horária:
</span></b><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun:
yes"> </span>102 h/a para 68 h/a teóricas  anual<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Seriação: </span></b><span
style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>da 4ª série para a
3ª série<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText style='text-align:justify;mso-outline-level:7'><span

<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
