<p class=MsoNormal align=center style='text-align:center'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>REGULAMENTO
DO COMPONENTE ESTÁGIO CURRICULAR SUPERVISIONADO DO CURSO DE GRADUAÇÃO EM
ENGENHARIA MECÂNICA<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center;mso-outline-level:
1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>TÍTULO
I<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center;mso-outline-level:
1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>Da
Caracterização</span></b><span style='color:windowtext'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center;mso-outline-level:
1'><span style='color:windowtext'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 1</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;</span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>O componente Estágio Curricular Supervisionado, doravante denominado
de Estágio, com carga horária de 272 horas, integrante do currículo do curso de
graduação em Engenharia Mecânica será realizado em indústrias ou instituições,
de acordo com as normas estabelecidas neste Regulamento, pela Resolução n</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;
mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:
Symbol'>°</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:38">027/2005</ins>-<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:38">CEP</ins> e pela legislação <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:38">federal </ins>vigente.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:0cm;mso-text-indent-alt:
35.45pt;mso-list:none;mso-list-ins:DEQ 20050711T0913'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>§ 1</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> A carga horária do Estágio, estabelecida pelo currículo
pleno do curso deverá ser integralizada ao longo do segundo semestre da quinta
série do curso.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:19">§ 2</ins></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:19"> A jornada
total de atividades em estágio, a ser cumprida pelo estagiário, deve</ins>rá<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:19"> compatibilizar-se com o seu
horário escolar e com o funcionamento da unidade concedente.<o:p></o:p></ins></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:0cm;mso-text-indent-alt:
35.45pt;mso-list:none;mso-list-ins:DEQ 20050711T0916'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:16">.</del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:16">§ </ins><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-11T09:19">3</ins></span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-char-type:
symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-char-type:symbol;
mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:16"> A jornada total não deve</ins><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:18">rá</ins><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-11T09:16"> ser inferior a </ins>272 horas, cumpridas em um
período não inferior a 100 dias, não podendo ser integralizada <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:16">de forma fracionada.<o:p></o:p></ins></span></p>

<h3 style='text-align:justify;text-indent:0cm;mso-text-indent-alt:35.45pt;
mso-list:none;mso-list-ins:DEQ 20050711T0919'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:19">§ 4</ins></span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;
mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:
Symbol'>°</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";font-weight:normal'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:19"> A jornada para o estágio </ins>deverá<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:19"> ser </ins>realizada em
conformidade com a Resolução n</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol;font-weight:normal'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";font-weight:normal'> 027/2005-CEP<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-11T09:19">.</ins><o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:1.0cm'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 2</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> O aluno poderá propor a realização de<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'> </b>carga horária excedente de Estágio de forma voluntária, a partir
da segunda série, podendo esta ser fracionada. <ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-11T09:19"><o:p></o:p></ins></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 3</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>O estágio realizar-se-á em unidades que desenvolvam
atividades de Engenharia Mecânica,<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-11T11:52"> que disponham de profissional com formaç</ins><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T11:53">ão teórico-prática na área do
estágio, preferencialmente Engenheiro Mecânico</ins>, e que tenham condições de
proporcionar experiência, aperfeiçoamento técnico, cultural, científico e de
relacionamento humano ao estagiário.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 4</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Os estagiários deverão desenvolver atividades previstas para
a área de Engenharia Mecânica, conforme Resolução n</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;
mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:
Symbol'>°</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> 218/1973 do Conselho
Federal de Engenharia, Arquitetura e Agronomia (CONFEA)<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T08:40">, ou a que venha substituí-la</ins>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 5</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Para a realização do estágio será necessária a existência de
instrumento jurídico celebrado entre a empresa ou instituição concedente e a
Universidade Estadual de Maringá (UEM), onde estarão acordadas todas as
condições para a realização do estágio.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center;mso-outline-level:
1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>TÍTULO
II<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Dos Objetivos<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 6</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>O estágio deve proporcionar ao estagiário a vivência de
situações profissionais nas diferentes áreas de atuação da Engenharia Mecânica,
bem como:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>a) possibilitar uma visão realista do funcionamento da
indústria ou <span style='letter-spacing:-.4pt'>instituição, bem como a
familiarização com seu futuro ambiente de trabalho;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText align=right style='text-align:right;mso-outline-level:
7'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>.../<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<table border=0 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style='border-collapse:collapse;
 mso-padding-alt:0cm 3.5pt 0cm 3.5pt'>
 <tr>
  <td width=515 valign=top style='width:386.25pt;padding:0cm 3.5pt 0cm 3.5pt'><span
  style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;
  mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
  mso-ansi-language:PT-BR;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br
  clear=all style='page-break-before:always'>
  </span>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
  normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.3pt'>/...
  Resolução nº 215/2005-CEP<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width=103 valign=top style='width:77.25pt;padding:0cm 3.5pt 0cm 3.5pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal align=right style='text-align:right'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
  normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.3pt'>fl. 10<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-indent:0cm;
line-height:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-indent:0cm;
line-height:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>b)&nbsp;propiciar
condições de treinamento específico pela aplicação, <span style='letter-spacing:
-.3pt'>aprimoramento e complementação dos conhecimentos adquiridos no curso;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-indent:0cm;
line-height:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>c) oferecer subsídios
à identificação de preferências em campos de futuras atividades profissionais;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-indent:0cm;
line-height:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>d) propiciar a
ampliação do interesse pela pesquisa científica e tecnológica relacionada com
os problemas peculiares às áreas de estágios;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-indent:0cm;
line-height:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.1pt'>e)
facilitar a aquisição de experiência específica em processos, métodos</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> e técnicas de produção;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='margin-left:35.45pt;text-indent:0cm;
line-height:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>f) ensejar
oportunidade para aplicação dos conhecimentos adquiridos, <span
style='letter-spacing:-.3pt'>com vistas a equacionar e resolver problemas
detectados pelo acadêmico.</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.4pt;line-height:normal'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 7</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Oferecer oportunidade de retroalimentação ao curso, visando
seu aprimoramento.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center;mso-outline-level:
1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>TÍTULO
III<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Da Organização<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.4pt;line-height:normal'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.2pt'>Art. 8</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:-.2pt;
mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-char-type:
symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.2pt'> </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.2pt'>A coordenação do componente Estágio
Curricular Supervisionado</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> <span
style='letter-spacing:-.1pt'>será exercida por um professor do curso de
graduação em Engenharia Mecânica, designado</span> pelo departamento <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:43">de lotação do</ins> curso de
Engenharia Mecânica.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>§ 1</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>O mandato do
coordenador de estágio será de dois anos, sendo permitida a recondução;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>§ 2</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> Para a atividade de coordenação deve ser definida uma carga
horária pelo departamento, de acordo com as normas vigentes na Instituição.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 9</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Para cada estagiário, o coordenador de estágio, indicará um
professor como orientador de estágio, e a empresa ou instituição concedente do
estágio indicará um<ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T09:23"> </ins><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-11T11:53">profissional</ins> como
supervisor de estágio.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center;mso-outline-level:
1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>TÍTULO
IV<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Da Elaboração, do Acompanhamento e da Avaliação<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.2pt'>Art. 10 </span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.2pt'>O estagiário deverá apresentar um plano de a<span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:52">Estágio </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:52">tividades</ins>, um relatório
parcial de atividades<ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:52"> </ins>e
um trabalho final,</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> conforme modelos e
normas estabelecidas pelo departamento <ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T08:43">de lotação do</ins> curso de graduação em
Engenharia Mecânica.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Parágrafo
único. </span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Para o Estagio
realizado com carga horária excedente, o estagiário deverá entregar apenas um
relatório final, a ser avaliado pelo orientador e supervisor.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.1pt'>Art. 11. </span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.1pt'>O plano de a<span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T08:53">Estágio </del></span></span><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
letter-spacing:-.2pt'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:53">tividades
</ins></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.1pt'>será
elaborado pelo estagiário em conjunto</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
com o supervisor de estágio na empresa ou instituição, sendo que este
encaminhará o mesmo ao coordenador e ao orientador de estágio.<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:55"><o:p></o:p></ins></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:0cm;mso-text-indent-alt:
35.4pt;mso-list:none;mso-list-ins:DEQ 20050721T0855'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-prop-change:
DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:55"><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>§ 1</span></ins></span></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:55"><span style='mso-prop-change:
DEQ 20050721T0857'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>O est</span></ins><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T08:56"><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>agiário
só poderá iniciar o estágio após a apr</span></ins><span style='mso-prop-change:
DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:59"><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>ovação</span></ins><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T08:56"><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'> do
</span></ins><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>p<span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:56"><span style='mso-prop-change:
DEQ 20050721T0857'>lano de </span></ins><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>a<span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:56"><span style='mso-prop-change:
DEQ 20050721T0857'>tividade<span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>s</span></span></ins><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T08:57"><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'> </span></ins><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>pelo<span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T08:57"><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'> </span></ins><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>c<span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T08:57"><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'>oordenador
de estágio</span></ins><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:58"><span style='mso-prop-change:
DEQ 20050721T0857'>.</span></ins><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:02"><span style='mso-prop-change:
DEQ 20050721T0857'><o:p></o:p></span></ins></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt;mso-list:none;
mso-list-ins:DEQ 20050721T0902'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:02">§ 2</ins></span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:02"><span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>O </ins>p<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:02">lano de </ins>a<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:02">tividades deve</ins>rá<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:02"> prever a elaboração d</ins>o<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:02"> </ins>r<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:02">elatório</ins><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:03"> </ins>p<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:03">arcial de </ins>a<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:03">tividades, obedecendo </ins><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:04">os prazos estabelecidos e</ins>m comum <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:04">acor</ins>d<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:04">o </ins>pelo<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:04"> </ins>o<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:04">rientador e estagiário.</ins><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>.../<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:02"><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]></del></span><span
style='mso-prop-change:DEQ 20050721T0857'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:02"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 12. </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>O estagiário deverá encaminhar o trabalho final ao
orientador nas datas previstas pelo calendário a ser estabelecido pelo <span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:54">Departamento </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:54">coordenador de estágio </ins><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:44">do</ins> curso de graduação em
Engenharia Mecânica, observado o Calendário Acadêmico da UEM.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.3pt'>Art. 13. </span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.3pt'>O departamento <ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:44">de
lotação do</ins> curso de graduação em Engenharia Mecânica</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> publicará em edital a relação dos estagiários que
procederam a entrega do trabalho final até a data prevista, definindo para cada
um a data, horário, local da defesa do trabalho final e a constituição da Banca
Examinadora.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent3 style='text-indent:35.45pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>§ 1</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>A Banca Examinadora
será constituída pelo orientador, que presidirá os trabalhos, e por <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:59">pelo menos </ins>dois professores
designados pelo c<ins cite="mailto:DEQ">oordenador de </ins>e<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ">stágio do </ins><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ">Departamento<span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></del></span>curso de graduação em Engenharia
Mecânica<ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:01">, podendo contar com
a participação de um profissional da área</ins>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.2pt'>§ 2</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:-.2pt;
mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-char-type:
symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.2pt'><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"> 
</span>A defesa do trabalho final deverá ser realizada em sessão pública<span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:01">,</del></span></span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:01"> respeitados os prazos acadêmicos do período letivo</del></span>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.1pt'>§ 3</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;letter-spacing:-.1pt;
mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-char-type:
symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.1pt'> O estagiário terá um prazo de até 15 dias
corridos, após a</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> defesa do trabalho
final, para efetuar as possíveis alterações sugeridas pelos membros da Banca
Examinadora e para encaminhar o trabalho corrigido definitivo <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:12">de acordo com as normas </ins>ao<span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:10"> presidente da
mesma</del></span><ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:10"> </ins>c<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:10">oordenador de </ins>e<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:10">stágio</ins>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent3 style='text-indent:35.45pt'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>§ 4</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:
Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span
style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'>°</span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> A nota do trabalho final será publicada somente após a
entrega do trabalho final corrigido, em sua versão definitiva.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.3pt'>Art. 14. </span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.3pt'>A verificação da aprendizagem obedecerá ao contido no critério</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> de avaliação do componente curricular aprovados pelo
departamento e colegiado de curso.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.45pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.4pt'>Parágrafo único</span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:
-.4pt'>. Tendo em vista as especificidades didático-pedagógicas</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> <span style='letter-spacing:-.2pt'>do componente
curricular, não haverá nova oportunidade, revisão de avaliação</span> e
realização de exame final, bem como não será permitido cursá-lo em dependência.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center;mso-outline-level:
1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>TÍTULO
V<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Das Atribuições<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art. 15. </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Ao coordenador do componente Estágio Curricular
Supervisionado compete:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>I&nbsp;-&nbsp;responder pelo estágio
junto ao departamento<ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13"> de
lotação do </ins>c<ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13">urso de </ins>graduação
em <ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13">Engenharia Mecânica</ins>;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13"><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>II
- propiciar o contato entre os acadêmicos e indústrias ou instituições, tendo
em vista a viabilização do Estágio Supervisionado;</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.2pt'><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13"><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>III - propor aos órgãos competentes
da Universidade Estadual de Maringá</del></span></span><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13"> celebração do
convênio/termo de compromisso;</del></span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13">IV</del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:13">II</ins>&nbsp;-&nbsp;realizar
reuniões periódicas com os estagiários e/ou com os orientadores;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:14">V - submeter ao Departamento<span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span>curso de Engenharia Mecânica a aprovação dos
nomes dos professores orientadores de estágio e demais componentes das bancas
examinadoras destinadas às avaliações dos trabalhos finais;</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:14"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:14">VI </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:14">III</ins>&nbsp;-&nbsp;estabelecer
datas para as avaliações previstas no critério de avaliação do componente
curricular;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:15">VII</del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:15">IV</ins>&nbsp;-&nbsp;confirmar a
aprovação <span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:14">final
</del></span>do estágio, tendo em seu poder o t<span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:15">relatório </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:15">rabalho </ins><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:15">f</del></span>final<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:15"> definitivo</ins><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:15"> sobre a situação
do acadêmico, encaminhado pelo professor orientador e o Trabalho Final
definitivo</del></span>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:16">VIII</del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:16"> V</ins>&nbsp;-&nbsp;encaminhar
ao departamento <ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:44">de lotação
do</ins> curso de graduação em Engenharia Mecânica os resultados das avaliações
previstas.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:36.0pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
letter-spacing:-.2pt'>Art. 16. </span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
letter-spacing:-.2pt'>Ao supervisor de estágio junto à indústria ou instituição
compete:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:-78.0pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>I&nbsp;-&nbsp;elaborar, em comum
acordo com o estagiário, o plano de <span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:16">estágio </del></span><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:16">atividades </ins>a ser cumprido;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:-78.0pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>II&nbsp;-&nbsp;orientar o estagiário
na elaboração do trabalho final;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText align=right style='text-align:right;mso-outline-level:
7'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span></span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.5pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>.../<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;

style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>III&nbsp;-&nbsp;acompanhar e
supervisionar a execução do plano de atividades de estágio;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:-78.0pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>IV&nbsp;-&nbsp;avaliar o rendimento
do estagiário durante a realização do estágio;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:-78.0pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.2pt'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>V&nbsp;-&nbsp;manter <span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:16">a coordenação </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:16">o </ins>o<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:17">rientador</ins><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:16"> </ins>de estágio <span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:17">informada </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:17">informado </ins>sobre o
desenvolvimento</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> das atividades do
estágio.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Art.
17. </span></b><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>Ao orientador de
estágio compete:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:17"><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>I
- propiciar às atividades de estágio, programadas em conjunto com os
supervisores nas indústrias/instituições, o imprescindível padrão qualitativo;</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:17"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>I&nbsp;-&nbsp;m<span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:17">realizar reuniões </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:17">anter contato </ins>com os estagiários
sob sua orientação;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>II&nbsp;-&nbsp;<span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">acompanhar e </del></span>avaliar
o trabalho desenvolvido pelo estagiário;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>III&nbsp;-&nbsp;participar das
reuniões convocadas pelo coordenador de estágio;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.2pt'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>IV&nbsp;-&nbsp;manter <span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">a coordenação </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">o </ins>c<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">oorde</ins>n<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">ador </ins><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">do </del></span><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">de </ins>estágio <span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">informada </del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:18">informado </ins>sobre o desenvolvimento</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'> das atividades do estágio;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>V&nbsp;-&nbsp;apresentar ao
coordenador de estágio o relatório de avaliação do estagiário nas datas
previstas pelo calendário a ser estabelecido pelo departamento <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T08:44">de lotação do</ins> curso de graduação
em Engenharia Mecânica, observado o Calendário Acadêmico da UEM.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.3pt'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>VI&nbsp;-&nbsp;presidir os trabalhos
da Banca Examinadora, por ocasião da avaliação</span><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>
do trabalho final.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
letter-spacing:-.4pt'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:19">Art. 17.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></del></span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.4pt'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19">Ao Departamento<span

"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"> compete:</del></span><span class=msoDel><del

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>   </span>I
- indicar o coordenador de estágios;</del></span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>   </span>II
- designar os professores orientadores;</del></span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>   </span>III
- aprovar a(s) vaga(s) de estágio, as quais deverão ser compatíveis com o
contexto básico da profissão de engenheiro mecânico.</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span

<p class=MsoBodyText2 align=center style='text-align:center;mso-outline-level:
1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:windowtext'>TÍTULO
VI<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>Dos Deveres <span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">e Direitos </del></span>do Estagiário<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal;tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal;tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">Capítulo I</del></span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal;tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">Dos Deveres</del></span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal;tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
style='mso-tab-count:1'>            </span>Art.<span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"> 18</del></span><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:19"> 1</ins>8. </span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>São deveres do estagiário, além dos previstos pel<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:20">a Resolução </ins>n</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-ascii-font-family:Arial;mso-hansi-font-family:Arial;mso-char-type:symbol;
mso-symbol-font-family:Symbol'><span style='mso-char-type:symbol;mso-symbol-font-family:
Symbol'>°</span></span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'> <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:20">027/2005</ins>-<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:20">CEP</ins>,<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:20"> d</ins>o Regimento Geral da UEM e pela legislação <ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:21">federal </ins>em vigor:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>I - cumprir este
Regulamento;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>II - observar e obedecer
as normas internas da indústria/instituição, bem como outras eventuais
recomendações ou requisitos ajustados entre as partes;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>III - participar da
elaboração do plano de<span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:21"> estágio</del></span><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:21"> atividades e cumpri-lo integralmente</ins>;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;tab-stops:0cm'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'>IV - manter contato constante com o orientador e com o
supervisor de estágio;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>V - manter elevado
padrão de comportamento e de relações humanas, condizentes com as atividades a
serem desenvolvidas;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>VI - comunicar e
justificar ao orientador e ao supervisor de <span style='letter-spacing:-.3pt'>estágio
na empresa ou instituição sua eventual ausência nas atividades</span> de
estágio;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'>VII - elaborar e
entregar ao orientador um relatório <span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:22">final </del></span><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:22">parcial </ins>de estágio<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:22"> e o </ins>t<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:22">rabalho </ins>f<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:22">inal</ins>, na forma, prazo e padrões
estabelecidos;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.45pt;tab-stops:0cm'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.2pt'>VIII - comparecer às reuniões
convocadas pelo orientador e/ou pelo coordenador de estágio;<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;mso-text-indent-alt:35.45pt;
line-height:normal;mso-list:none;mso-list-change:"%1\:12\:4\:\)" DEQ 20050721T0911;
tab-stops:0cm'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";letter-spacing:-.2pt'>IX
- encaminhar<span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:24">ao coordenador de estágio do Departamento </del></span></span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:24"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"> </span>curso de
Engenharia Mecânica</del></span><ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:24"> </ins>à<ins cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:24"> coordenação geral de estágio</ins>, p<span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:24">pedido de estágio
</del></span><ins cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:24">lano de </ins>a<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:24">tividades </ins><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:25">aprovados pelo </ins>o<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:25">rientador e pelo </ins>s<ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:25">upervisor de est</ins><ins
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">ágio </ins>antes do seu início.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='margin-left:53.4pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;
line-height:normal;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo6;mso-list-change:"%1\:13\:4\:\)" DEQ 20050721T0911;
tab-stops:0cm list 18.0pt 71.4pt'><![if !supportLists]><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:25">a)</del></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:25">enviar ao professor orientador o plano de estágio.</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:25"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">Capítulo II</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">Dos Direitos</del></span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]></del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-align:justify;text-indent:35.4pt'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">Art. 19.<span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></del></span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">São direitos do estagiário, além de outros assegurados
pelo Regimento Geral da Universidade Estadual de Maringá e pela legislação em
vigor :</del></span><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.4pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">a) dispor de elementos necessários à execução de
suas atividades, </del></span><span style='letter-spacing:-.4pt'><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">dentro das
possibilidades científicas, técnicas e financeiras da Universidade;</del></span></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.4pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">b) receber orientação necessária para realizar as
atividades do estágio dentro da opção escolhida;</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.4pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">c) ser encaminhado para a realização do estágio;</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.4pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">d) ser esclarecido sobre os convênios firmados para
a realização de seu estágio;</del></span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.4pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">e) conhecer a programação das atividades a serem
desenvolvidas no Estágio Supervisionado;</del></span><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.4pt;text-align:justify'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">f) apresentar propostas ou sugestões que possam
contribuir para o aprimoramento das atividades de estágio.</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyText2 style='mso-outline-level:1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><u><span style='color:windowtext'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">TÍTULO VIII</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></u></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 align=center style='text-align:center;text-indent:
0cm;line-height:normal;mso-outline-level:1'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del
cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">Da Solicitação da Vaga de Estágio</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:0cm;line-height:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><![if !supportEmptyParas]>&nbsp;<![endif]></del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.4pt;line-height:normal'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">Art. 20.<span
style="mso-spacerun: yes">  </span></del></span></span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">A solicitação da vaga de estágio dar-se-á por
intermédio da coordenação de estágios do Departamento<span style="mso-spacerun:
yes">  </span>curso de Engenharia Mecânica, para o que se exigirá do acadêmico:</del></span><span
class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ" datetime="2005-07-21T09:26"><o:p></o:p></del></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.4pt;line-height:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman"'><span class=msoDel><del cite="mailto:DEQ"
datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">I - preenchimento da ficha de solicitação de
estágio, disponível na </del></span><span style='letter-spacing:-.1pt'><span

datetime="2005-07-21T09:26">anexando o seu currículo, controle curricular e
horário de disponibilidade para</del></span></span><span class=msoDel><del

<p class=MsoBodyTextIndent2 style='text-indent:35.4pt;line-height:normal'><span
